320→export class AutoIndentOnPasteCommand implements ICommand {\n   321→\n   322→\tprivate readonly _edits: { range: IRange; text: string; eol?: EndOfLineSequence }[];\n   323→\n   324→\tprivate readonly _initialSelection: Selection;\n   325→\tprivate _selectionId: string | null;\n   326→\n   327→\tconstructor(edits: TextEdit[], initialSelection: Selection) {\n   328→\t\tthis._initialSelection = initialSelection;\n   329→\t\tthis._edits = [];\n   330→\t\tthis._selectionId = null;\n   331→\n   332→\t\tfor (const edit of edits) {\n   333→\t\t\tif (edit.range && typeof edit.text === 'string') {\n   334→\t\t\t\tthis._edits.push(edit as { range: IRange; text: string; eol?: EndOfLineSequence });\n   335→\t\t\t}\n   336→\t\t}\n   337→\t}\n   338→\n   339→\tpublic getEditOperations(model: ITextModel, builder: IEditOperationBuilder): void {\n   340→\t\tfor (const edit of this._edits) {\n   341→\t\t\tbuilder.addEditOperation(Range.lift(edit.range), edit.text);\n   342→\t\t}\n   343→\n   344→\t\tlet selectionIsSet = false;\n   345→\t\tif (Array.isArray(this._edits) && this._edits.length === 1 && this._initialSelection.isEmpty()) {\n   346→\t\t\tif (this._edits[0].range.startColumn === this._initialSelection.endColumn &&\n   347→\t\t\t\tthis._edits[0].range.startLineNumber === this._initialSelection.endLineNumber) {\n   348→\t\t\t\tselectionIsSet = true;\n   349→\t\t\t\tthis._selectionId = builder.trackSelection(this._initialSelection, true);\n   350→\t\t\t} else if (this._edits[0].range.endColumn === this._initialSelection.startColumn &&\n   351→\t\t\t\tthis._edits[0].range.endLineNumber === this._initialSelection.startLineNumber) {\n   352→\t\t\t\tselectionIsSet = true;\n   353→\t\t\t\tthis._selectionId = builder.trackSelection(this._initialSelection, false);\n   354→\t\t\t}\n   355→\t\t}\n   356→\n   357→\t\tif (!selectionIsSet) {\n   358→\t\t\tthis._selectionId = builder.trackSelection(this._initialSelection);\n   359→\t\t}\n   360→\t}\n   361→\n   362→\tpublic computeCursorState(model: ITextModel, helper: ICursorStateComputerData): Selection {\n   363→\t\treturn helper.getTrackedSelection(this._selectionId!);\n   364→\t}\n   365→}\n   366→\n   367→export class AutoIndentOnPaste implements IEditorContribution {\n   368→\tpublic static readonly ID = 'editor.contrib.autoIndentOnPaste';\n   369→\n   370→\tprivate readonly callOnDispose = new DisposableStore();\n   371→\tprivate readonly callOnModel = new DisposableStore();\n   372→\n   373→\tconstructor(\n   374→\t\tprivate readonly editor: ICodeEditor,\n   375→\t\t@ILanguageConfigurationService private readonly _languageConfigurationService: ILanguageConfigurationService\n   376→\t) {\n   377→\n   378→\t\tthis.callOnDispose.add(editor.onDidChangeConfiguration(() => this.update()));\n   379→\t\tthis.callOnDispose.add(editor.onDidChangeModel(() => this.update()));\n   380→\t\tthis.callOnDispose.add(editor.onDidChangeModelLanguage(() => this.update()));\n   381→\t}\n   382→\n   383→\tprivate update(): void {\n   384→\n   385→\t\t// clean up\n   386→\t\tthis.callOnModel.clear();\n   387→\n   388→\t\t// we are disabled\n   389→\t\tif (this.editor.getOption(EditorOption.autoIndent) < EditorAutoIndentStrategy.Full || this.editor.getOption(EditorOption.formatOnPaste)) {\n   390→\t\t\treturn;\n   391→\t\t}\n   392→\n   393→\t\t// no model\n   394→\t\tif (!this.editor.hasModel()) {\n   395→\t\t\treturn;\n   396→\t\t}\n   397→\n   398→\t\tthis.callOnModel.add(this.editor.onDidPaste(({ range }) => {\n   399→\t\t\tthis.trigger(range);\n   400→\t\t}));\n   401→\t}\n   402→\n   403→\tpublic trigger(range: Range): void {\n   404→\t\tconst selections = this.editor.getSelections();\n   405→\t\tif (selections === null || selections.length > 1) {\n   406→\t\t\treturn;\n   407→\t\t}\n   408→\n   409→\t\tconst model = this.editor.getModel();\n   410→\t\tif (!model) {\n   411→\t\t\treturn;\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t\tconst containsOnlyWhitespace = this.rangeContainsOnlyWhitespaceCharacters(model, range);\n   414→\t\tif (containsOnlyWhitespace) {\n   415→\t\t\treturn;\n   416→\t\t}\n   417→\t\tif (isStartOrEndInString(model, range)) {\n   418→\t\t\treturn;\n   419→\t\t}\n   420→\t\tif (!model.tokenization.isCheapToTokenize(range.getStartPosition().lineNumber)) {\n   421→\t\t\treturn;\n   422→\t\t}\n   423→\t\tconst autoIndent = this.editor.getOption(EditorOption.autoIndent);\n   424→\t\tconst { tabSize, indentSize, insertSpaces } = model.getOptions();\n   425→\t\tconst textEdits: TextEdit[] = [];\n   426→\n   427→\t\tconst indentConverter = {\n   428→\t\t\tshiftIndent: (indentation: string) => {\n   429→\t\t\t\treturn ShiftCommand.shiftIndent(indentation, indentation.length + 1, tabSize, indentSize, insertSpaces);\n   430→\t\t\t},\n   431→\t\t\tunshiftIndent: (indentation: string) => {\n   432→\t\t\t\treturn ShiftCommand.unshiftIndent(indentation, indentation.length + 1, tabSize, indentSize, insertSpaces);\n   433→\t\t\t}\n   434→\t\t};\n   435→\n   436→\t\tlet startLineNumber = range.startLineNumber;\n   437→\n   438→\t\twhile (startLineNumber <= range.endLineNumber) {\n   439→\t\t\tif (this.shouldIgnoreLine(model, startLineNumber)) {\n   440→\t\t\t\tstartLineNumber++;\n   441→\t\t\t\tcontinue;\n   442→\t\t\t}\n   443→\t\t\tbreak;\n   444→\t\t}\n   445→\n   446→\t\tif (startLineNumber > range.endLineNumber) {\n   447→\t\t\treturn;\n   448→\t\t}\n   449→\n   450→\t\tlet firstLineText = model.getLineContent(startLineNumber);\n   451→\t\tif (!/\\S/.test(firstLineText.substring(0, range.startColumn - 1))) {\n   452→\t\t\tconst indentOfFirstLine = getGoodIndentForLine(autoIndent, model, model.getLanguageId(), startLineNumber, indentConverter, this._languageConfigurationService);\n   453→\n   454→\t\t\tif (indentOfFirstLine !== null) {\n   455→\t\t\t\tconst oldIndentation = strings.getLeadingWhitespace(firstLineText);\n   456→\t\t\t\tconst newSpaceCnt = indentUtils.getSpaceCnt(indentOfFirstLine, tabSize);\n   457→\t\t\t\tconst oldSpaceCnt = indentUtils.getSpaceCnt(oldIndentation, tabSize);\n   458→\n   459→\t\t\t\tif (newSpaceCnt !== oldSpaceCnt) {\n   460→\t\t\t\t\tconst newIndent = indentUtils.generateIndent(newSpaceCnt, tabSize, insertSpaces);\n   461→\t\t\t\t\ttextEdits.push({\n   462→\t\t\t\t\t\trange: new Range(startLineNumber, 1, startLineNumber, oldIndentation.length + 1),\n   463→\t\t\t\t\t\ttext: newIndent\n   464→\t\t\t\t\t});\n   465→\t\t\t\t\tfirstLineText = newIndent + firstLineText.substring(oldIndentation.length);\n   466→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   467→\t\t\t\t\tconst indentMetadata = getIndentMetadata(model, startLineNumber, this._languageConfigurationService);\n   468→\n   469→\t\t\t\t\tif (indentMetadata === 0 || indentMetadata === IndentConsts.UNINDENT_MASK) {\n   470→\t\t\t\t\t\t// we paste content into a line where only contains whitespaces\n   471→\t\t\t\t\t\t// after pasting, the indentation of the first line is already IndentRangeProvider\n**Location:** `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/indentRangeProvider.ts`\n\n- **ID:** `'indent'`\n- **Purpose:** Calculates folding regions based on indentation levels\n- **Key Features:**\n  - Uses `computeRanges()` function that analyzes indentation\n  - Supports `FoldingMarkers` (regex patterns for `#region`/`#endregion`)\n  - Handles off-side rule for languages like Python\n  - Implements `RangesCollector` to gather and optimize ranges\n  - Respects folding limits with `FoldingLimitReporter`\n\n#### B. Region Names/Labels - Current Architecture\n\n**Current Limitations:**\n- VS Code's current folding system **does NOT store region names/labels**\n- Region markers like `// #region MyName` are detected and used to create folds, but the `MyName` part is **not extracted or stored**\n- Only the region's start and end lines plus the region type/kind are stored\n\n**Markers Definition:**\n```typescript\nexport interface FoldingMarkers {\n    start: RegExp;  // e.g., /^\\s*#region\\b/\n    end: RegExp;    // e.g., /^\\s*#endregion\\b/\n}\n```\n\nExample from language configuration:\n```typescript\nconst markers: FoldingMarkers = {\n    start: /^\\s*#region\\b/,\n    end: /^\\s*#endregion\\b/\n};\n```\n\n**How Markers Work:**\n- Located in `languageConfiguration.ts` under `FoldingRules`\n- Defined per language in their language configuration\n- Used by `IndentRangeProvider.computeRanges()` to identify region boundaries\n- Applied as regex matching on line content, ignoring the portion after matching\n\n### 5. Create start/end index arrays\n        const startIndexes = new Uint32Array([...]);\n        const endIndexes = new Uint32Array([...]);\n        const types = ['region', 'comment', ...];\n        \n        // 3. Return FoldingRegions\n        return new FoldingRegions(startIndexes, endIndexes, types);\n    }\n    \n    dispose() {\n        // Cleanup resources\n    }\n}\n```\n\n2. **Register Provider:**\n- Providers are registered via `FoldingRangeProvider` interface with language features service\n- `SyntaxRangeProvider` will wrap and use your provider automatically\n\n3. **Handle Limits:**\n- Use `FoldingLimitReporter` to track and respect region count limits\n- Call `foldingRangesLimit.update(computed, limited)` to report status\n\n### 6.
